msg:Let me talk about the location first. The hotel is located on Sanya Bay Road. Just across the road, there is a beach opposite. You can enjoy the sunset of Sanya Bay. Strolling along the Coconut Dream Corridor is refreshing. The Chinese-style buildings of the hotel not only remind me of the ancient "Afang Palace"... Let me talk about the two surprises the hotel gave me: the Mini room is small but fully functional. A 1.5-meter-long bed, a balcony and a separate bathroom are enough for a solo traveler like me; the hotel's swimming pool is also a highlight. It is rectangular and 1.5 meters deep. You should know that most resort hotel swimming pools are polygonal and only 1.2 to 1.4 meters deep. Swimming pools like Sanya Bay Guest House are extremely rare. The hotel's breakfast includes Hainan specialties such as Baoluo noodles and Hainan pickled noodles. Don't forget to taste them. As for the noise of airplanes taking off and landing, I completely ignore it. The big sister in charge of room hygiene is conscientious; special thanks to Fei'er at the front desk, who called me in advance to ask if I have any needs and inform me of relevant matters. In short, it is cost-effective and highly recommended.

The seaside barbecue environment is good and tastes good. I really can‚Äôt do it, but the scenery is beautiful, so just treat it as an environment to eat. When you sit by the swimming pool at night, a staff member comes forward to spray mosquito repellent. If you have a takeaway in your hand that is inconvenient to carry, the restaurant waiter will hand you the bag. As long as you look confused, the staff will come over to ask. The service is far better than that of family hotels in Haitang Bay and Yalong Bay, not to mention the exclusive beach scenery, and it is very convenient to travel. The price/performance ratio is unbeatable at less than 500 per night.

msg:In 1960, the country was plunged into a deep famine and economic crisis, but at this time, various provinces and cities were keen on large-scale construction projects and rushing to build palaces or guest houses. At that time, Tao Zhu, who was in charge of Guangdong Province and the first secretary of the Guangdong Provincial Party Committee, went to Hainan Island to inspect work. He immediately took a fancy to the geomantic treasure land called Yezhuang at the foot of Luhuitou Mountain: surrounded by the sea on three sides, with beautiful mountains and jade. Like coconut groves, and white jade-like beaches. Tao Zhu immediately instructed to allocate funds to build a guest house here. The guest house started construction in 1959 and was officially opened for business in 1961, named Yezhuang Guest House. It mainly receives distinguished guests from central leaders and dignitaries from various countries.
Building No. 1 of Yezhuang Guest House is the main building. It is a one-story bungalow with a cloister and a construction area of ‚Äã‚Äã300 square meters. It is located in the south of Yezhuang compound. Zhou Enlai (1960s), Liu Shaoqi, Deng Xiaoping (1960s), Ye Jianying, Party and state leaders such as Chen Yi (1960s), Xie Juezai, Dong Biwu, Wang Zhen, Guo Moruo, Zhang Aiping (1985), Jiang Zemin (1988), as well as foreign heads of state such as Ho Chi Minh and Sihanouk, and international leaders such as Snow and Ma Haide A friend once stayed here.
In 1970, it was renamed Luhuitou Guesthouse. In 2009, due to the age of the original building, it was decided to attract inves**ent and rebuild with the approval of Hainan Province. Finally, the Banyan Tree Group was selected to fund the reconstruction of the original site and set aside a piece of land to build the Banyan Tree Hotel and operate it for me. , Luhuitou State Guesthouse and Banyan Tree Hotel were built in 2010. It covers an area of ‚Äã‚Äã69 acres and has a total construction area of ‚Äã‚Äã31,700 square meters. Changed its name to Luhuitou State Guesthouse.
Time and space can change at any time, and continue to write wonderful stories. Today, Sanya Luhuitou State Guesthouse has 260 guest rooms/suites, divided into state guest area and business resort area. The state guest area includes four presidential villas and nine ministerial villas; the business resort area has more than 180 luxury guest rooms. The hotel has a lobby bar, Chinese restaurant, Western restaurant, KTV box, multi-functional banquet hall, small conference room, SPA, swimming pool, tea bar and other comprehensive supporting facilities. In addition, the hotel has a unique coastline with shallow embankment artificial beach, 487-meter trestle and The viewing platform allows you to enjoy the charm of the sea, mountains and gardens.

Here, you can enjoy a luxurious and comfortable sea view room; bathe in the tropical style of the coastal city; experience the exquisite and elegant Western culture; taste the pure Hainan style; overlook the Luhuitou Ridge surrounded by green mountains and clear waters; and be intoxicated by the mountains and the sea. It's pleasant to come. At the foot of Qingshan Mountain, you will not only get the waves and magnificence of the sea, but also the touching beautiful legend of Luhuitou.

Located at the foot of the Luhuitou Mountains, facing the South China Sea in the front and Qingshan Mountain in the back, it can be described as a place with beautiful mountains and clear waters and outstanding people. Luhuitou State Guesthouse is a very quiet star resort hotel! There is also leadership-level service quality, a long history and cultural background, and being adjacent to the central leadership, a sense of pride arises, far surpassing many big-name hotels.
